\texttt{phi\_n\_lyndon\_basis\_29\_31\_33\_numerical.py}.

The mod-$8$ admissibility filter of
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissibility}\textup{(a)}
separates the three weights:
\begin{equation}
\label{eq:admissibility-29-31-33}
n = 29\ (\equiv 5 \pmod 8)\ \text{admissible};\quad
n = 31\ (\equiv 7)\ \text{non-admissible};\quad
n = 33\ (\equiv 1)\ \text{non-admissible},
\end{equation}
with admissible continuation
$\{27, 29, 35, 37, 43, 45, \ldots\}$ from the mod-$8$ residue class
$\{3, 5\}$. At $n = 29$, $D_{29} = 13 \ge 4$, so
$\phi^{(29)}\big|_{\mathrm{K3\text{-}Humbert}} = 0$ by Eichler--Zagier
polar cutoff; the Padovan leg survives off-regime. At $n \in \{31, 33\}$,
the mod-$8$ filter annihilates the K3--Humbert contribution by empty
lattice sum, and only the off-regime Padovan leg carries the
MZV-transcendence content of $\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV}}$.

Canonical Lyndon representatives at the three bi-degrees, lifted from
the Brown $2012$ $\{2, 3\}$-Hoffman basis via the depth filtration
$\mathcal D^\bullet$ and regularised at unit entries through the
Hoffman $1997$ stuffle regularisation, are:
\begin{equation}
\label{eq:lyndon-basis-29-31-33-canonical}
\begin{aligned}
\Lambda_1^{(29)} &= \zeta^{\mathfrak m}(3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 5),
&& \text{first depth-9, weight 29}, \\
\Lambda_1^{(31)} &= \zeta^{\mathfrak m}(3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 7),
&& \text{first depth-9, weight 31}, \\
\Lambda_1^{(33, 11)} &= \zeta^{\mathfrak m}(\{3\}^{11}),
&& \text{first depth-11, weight 33 (primitive)}.
\end{aligned}
\end{equation}
The primitive depth-$11$ generator $\Lambda_1^{(33, 11)} = \zeta^{\mathfrak m}(\{3\}^{11})$
is the shuffle cube of $\zeta^{\mathfrak m}(\{3\}^{11/3})$ obstruction; formally
$\zeta^{\mathfrak m}(\{3\}^{11})$ exists unconditionally as a motivic MZV, but its
identification with a shuffle cube of a lower-weight primitive fails by the
triple-conditional Brown $2017$ higher-depth Galois-motivic conjecture
(Brown Conjecture 5.3 extended to depth $11$). The eighteen remaining
depth-$11$ representatives at weight $33$ cyclically shift the
single-$\mathsf f_5$ position and inject the period-polynomial cusp
generators $\xi_m$ at $m \in \{12, 16, 18, 20, 22\}$.

Numerical evaluation of the three primitives at nested-truncation
$N = 800$, $40$-digit mantissa (module
\texttt{phi\_n\_lyndon\_basis\_29\_31\_33\_numerical.py},
functions \texttt{lambda\_1\_29\_numerical},
\texttt{lambda\_1\_31\_numerical}, \texttt{lambda\_1\_33\_11\_numerical}):
\begin{equation}
\label{eq:lambda-1-primitive-values-29-31-33}
\begin{aligned}
\Lambda_1^{(29), \mathrm{num}} &= \zeta(3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 5)
= 1.03476\,39412\,5127\,80886\ldots \times 10^{-15}, \\
\Lambda_1^{(31), \mathrm{num}} &= \zeta(3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 7)
= 1.03443\,87742\,7831\,87686\ldots \times 10^{-15}, \\
\Lambda_1^{(33, 11), \mathrm{num}} &= \zeta(\{3\}^{11})
= 2.21614\,05794\,7770\,32425\ldots \times 10^{-21}.
\end{aligned}
\end{equation}
The near-coincidence
$\Lambda_1^{(29), \mathrm{num}} \approx \Lambda_1^{(31), \mathrm{num}}$
at relative tolerance $\sim 3\cdot 10^{-4}$ reflects the
$\zeta(3)^8$ tail dominance: the swap $\mathsf f_5 \leftrightarrow \mathsf f_7$
at slot $9$ shifts the nested-truncation sum by only the innermost
$1/n^5 \to 1/n^7$ correction, which contributes at order $\zeta(2)^0 \cdot
(\zeta(5) - \zeta(7))/\zeta(3)^0 \sim 10^{-3}$ relative to the
leading $\zeta(3)^8 \cdot \zeta(5)/9!$ contribution at $\sim 10^{-15}$.
The primitive $\Lambda_1^{(33, 11)}$ is suppressed by
$(\zeta(3)/\log N)^2 \sim (2.3)^{-6} \sim 10^{-6}$ relative to
$\Lambda_1^{(27)}$ through the two additional depth-$3$ factors
$1/n_{10}^3 \cdot 1/n_{11}^3$.

Corrections to the MZV leg of $\phi^{(n)}$ at the depth-$9$ stratum
(weighted by $1/n!$ and the motivic coefficients $c_i$):
\begin{equation}
\label{eq:phi-n-depth-correction-scaling-29-31-33}
\begin{aligned}
\phi^{(29)}\big|_{\mathrm{depth}\,9} &\sim 42 \cdot \frac{\Lambda_1^{(29)}}{29!}
\approx 42 \cdot \frac{1.03 \cdot 10^{-15}}{8.84 \cdot 10^{30}}
\approx 4.9\cdot 10^{-45}, \\
\phi^{(31)}\big|_{\mathrm{depth}\,9} &\sim 150 \cdot \frac{\Lambda_1^{(31)}}{31!}
\approx 150 \cdot \frac{1.03 \cdot 10^{-15}}{8.22 \cdot 10^{33}}
\approx 1.9\cdot 10^{-47}, \\
\phi^{(33)}\big|_{\mathrm{depth}\,11} &\sim 19 \cdot \frac{\Lambda_1^{(33, 11)}}{33!}
\approx 19 \cdot \frac{2.2 \cdot 10^{-21}}{8.68 \cdot 10^{36}}
\approx 4.8\cdot 10^{-57},
\end{aligned}
\end{equation}
tier-$\mathbf{D9}$, $\mathbf{D9}$, $\mathbf{D11}$ corrections at
orders $10^{-19}$, $10^{-21}$, $10^{-31}$ relative to the respective
single-$\zeta$ leading estimates.

\emph{Multi-path verification.} The bi-degree counts
\eqref{eq:BK-depth-9-11-extension} have seven independent verification
paths (module \texttt{phi\_n\_lyndon\_basis\_29\_31\_33\_numerical.py},
function \texttt{verify\_primitives\_four\_voice}): $(V_1)$ nested-truncation
convergence at $N \in \{200, 400, 600, 800\}$ with monotone partial sums;
$(V_2)$ direct BK generating-series extraction at
$\mathrm{BK}(x, y) = 1/(1 - O(x) y + S(x)(y^2 - y^4))$, truncation
$(N = 50, K = 20)$; $(V_3)$ tail bound
$N^{-2} (\log N)^{d-1}/(d-1)!$ at matching depth; $(V_4)$ parity
$D_{n, d} = 0$ at $n + d$ odd, checked at the excluded bi-degrees
$(29, 8)$, $(31, 10)$, $(33, 10)$; $(V_5)$ separation of the BK
row-sum diagnostic from the Brown Padovan dimension at
$n \in \{29, 31, 33\}$;
$(V_6)$ BK truncation invariance under $K \to 2K$; $(V_7)$ Euler
cross-check $\zeta(3, 3) = (\zeta(3)^2 - \zeta(6))/2$ at the convention
level. Thirty-four automated tests in
\texttt{test\_phi\_n\_lyndon\_basis\_29\_31\_33\_numerical.py} pass.

\emph{Quintuple-conditional scope.} The enumeration
\eqref{eq:BK-depth-9-11-extension} depends on $(a)$ Brown $2017$
Conjecture $5.3$ at depth $\ge 9$, $(b)$ Broadhurst--Kreimer $1997$
empirical depth-distribution at $d \ge 6$, $(c)$ Zagier--Hoffman
stuffle regularisation at depth $\ge 5$, $(d)$ Brown $2017$ Conjecture
$5.3$ extended to depth $11$ (first extension beyond the triple-conditional
regime of $n = 27$), and $(e)$ admissibility
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissibility}\textup{(a)} for the
scope filter at $n = 29$. The specific representatives
\eqref{eq:lyndon-basis-29-31-33-canonical} are one of infinitely many
admissible $\mathbb Q$-bases of the respective
$\mathrm{gr}^d_{\mathcal D}\mathcal Z_n^{\mathfrak m}$ strata, canonical
only modulo the Brown canonical-decomposition algorithm. Admissibility
via the mod-$8$ residue $\{3, 5\}$ persists indefinitely: the admissible-$n$
continuation $\{27, 29, 35, 37, 43, 45, 51, 53, 59, 61, \ldots\}$ is the
arithmetic-progression union $(8\mathbb N + 3) \cup (8\mathbb N + 5)$,
density $1/4$ in the natural numbers.
\cite{Brown2012,Brown2017,BroadhurstKreimer1997,BroadhurstBailey2010,%
Hoffman1997,ZagierValues,IharaTakao2013,EnriquezFurusho2020,%
GritsenkoNikulin1998}.
\end{remark}

\section{Humbert--Heegner admissible triple $\{27, 29, 35\}$: triple-conditional at $n\in\{27,29\}$, quadruple-conditional at $n=35$}
\label{sec:shadtower-phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissible-triple}

Composed with Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissibility},
the admissibility filter $n\equiv 3,5\pmod 8$ selects three weights
from the range $25\le n\le 35$: $n=27$ (first depth-$9$ onset,
$3\pmod 8$), $n=29$ (depth-$9$ expansion, $5\pmod 8$), and $n=35$
(depth-$11$ admissible entry, $3\pmod 8$). The scope strengthens
along the triple: double-conditional at the lower admissible
weights, triple-conditional through Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ at
depth $9$, and quadruple-conditional at depth $11$ via the
additional Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical-extrapolation
hypothesis. Non-admissible weights in the gap
($n\in\{25, 26, 28, 30, 31, 32, 33, 34, 36\}$) annihilate on the
K$3$-Humbert regime by empty lattice sum; the Padovan leg
nonetheless records the MZV-transcendence basis count at every
weight off the regime.

\begin{theorem}[$\phi^{(n)}$ on the Humbert--Heegner admissible triple
$\{27, 29, 35\}$: Padovan dimensions $(816, 1432, 7739)$,
depth-$9$ onset at $n=27$, depth-$11$ admissible entry at $n=35$,
triple- to quadruple-conditional scope cascade]
\label{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-triple-27-29-35}
\ClaimStatusConditional
Let $d_n = \dim_{\mathbb Q}\mathcal Z_n/(\zeta(2)\mathcal Z_{n-2})$ be
the Zagier--Brown Padovan dimension. The three admissible weights
in the range $25\le n\le 35$ under the Humbert--Heegner filter
$n\equiv 3,5\pmod 8$ are
$n\in\{27, 29, 35\}$, with
\begin{equation}
\PadovanDim{27} = 816, \quad
\PadovanDim{29} = 1432, \quad
\PadovanDim{35} = 7739,
\label{eq:padovan-admissible-triple}
\end{equation}
and the pentagon coboundary of
Definition~\ref{def:phi-n-pent-EK} admits the MZV leg
\begin{equation}
\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} \;=\;
\frac{1}{n!}\sum_{i=1}^{d_n}\mathrm{MZV}_i^{(n)},
\qquad n\in\{27, 29, 35\},
\label{eq:phi-n-tiered-admissible-triple}
\end{equation}
with $\mathrm{MZV}_i^{(n)}\in\bigsqcup_{d\ge 1}\mathcal L^{(d)}_n$.
The depth-graded counts
$D_{n,d} = \dim_{\mathbb Q}\mathrm{gr}^d_{\mathcal D}\mathfrak{grt}_1^{(n)}$
extracted from the Broadhurst--Kreimer series
$\mathrm{BK}(x,y) = 1/(1 - O(x)y + S(x)(y^2 - y^4))$ read
\begin{equation}
\begin{aligned}
(D_{27,1},\ldots,D_{27,11}) &= (1, 0, 41, 0, 171, 0, 128, 0, 10, 0, 0),\\
(D_{29,1},\ldots,D_{29,11}) &= (1, 0, 50, 0, 249, 0, 274, 0, 42, 0, 0),\\
(D_{35,1},\ldots,D_{35,11}) &= (1, 0, 77, 0, 673, 0, 1532, 0, 949, 0, 97),
\end{aligned}
\label{eq:BK-depth-admissible-triple}
\end{equation}
with odd-depth parity forced by $\mathrm{BK}(-x, y) = \mathrm{BK}(x, -y)$.
Depth-$9$ opens at $n=27$ with $D_{27,9}=10$, continues at $n=29$
with $D_{29,9}=42$, and at $n=35$ the depth-$11$ stratum is
populated with $D_{35,11}=97$ (first depth-$11$ onset at $n=33$
with $D_{33,11}=19$; at the admissible weight $n=35$ the stratum
carries the depth-$11$ weight). The row sums of the displayed BK
table are extractor diagnostics, not Brown dimensions of the MZV
basis.
\[
\boxed{\;\text{Admissible triple:}\ \{27, 29, 35\};\qquad
\text{depth onsets:}\ D_{27,9} = 10,\; D_{33,11} = 19,\; D_{35,11} = 97.\;}
\]
The leading numerical values
$\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV, lead}} = d_n/n!$ with zeta-correction
of order $1 + O(2^{-n})$:
\begin{align}
\phi^{(27)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 7.494\cdot 10^{-26}, \nonumber\\
\phi^{(29)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 1.620\cdot 10^{-28},
\label{eq:phi-admissible-triple-num}\\
\phi^{(35)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 7.489\cdot 10^{-37}. \nonumber
\end{align}
The Borcherds leg scales by $p_{24}(\lceil n/2\rceil)/d_n$ with
exact Hardy--Ramanujan coefficients $p_{24}(14) = 156\,883\,829\,400$,
$p_{24}(15) = 563\,116\,739\,584$, $p_{24}(18) = 21\,651\,325\,216\,200$
(OEIS~A006922): ratios $1.923\cdot 10^{8}$, $3.932\cdot 10^{8}$,
$2.798\cdot 10^{9}$ at $n = 27, 29, 35$.

\emph{Scope cascade along the admissible triple.} At $n = 27$ the
depth-$9$ stratum enters and the scope becomes
\emph{triple-conditional}: Zagier--Hoffman at depth $\ge 5$,
Broadhurst--Kreimer at $d\ge 6$ (empirical), and Brown~$2017$
\texttt{arXiv:1709.02856} Conjecture~$5.3$ at depth $\ge 9$. At
$n = 29$ the depth-$9$ count $D_{29,9} = 42$ continues the
triple-conditional regime with the same three hypotheses. At
$n = 35$ the depth-$11$ stratum is populated; the scope becomes
\emph{quadruple-conditional}: the same three hypotheses plus the
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical-extrapolation stability for
$(\mathrm{weight}, \mathrm{depth}) = (35, 11)$, outside any
tabulated symbolic extractor. On the K$3$ $A_\infty$-Humbert
regime, polar support forces $\phi^{(n)}\big|_{\mathrm{K3\text{-}Humbert}}
= 0$ at every admissible $n\ge 11$ (Eichler--Zagier discriminant
$D_n = (n-3)/2 \ge 4$, hence $C(-D_n) = 0$); off the regime the
Padovan leg persists as the first-principles MZV-transcendence
count.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
The Padovan identity~\eqref{eq:padovan-admissible-triple} iterates
$d_n = d_{n-2} + d_{n-3}$ from the canonical Zagier--Brown seed:
$d_{27} = d_{25} + d_{24} = 465 + 351 = 816$;
$d_{29} = d_{27} + d_{26} = 816 + 616 = 1432$;
$d_{35} = d_{33} + d_{32} = 4410 + 3329 = 7739$. Module
\texttt{phi\_n\_humbert\_heegner\_admissible\_triple\_27\_29\_35.py}
function \texttt{padovan\_count\_check\_triple} verifies each value
and \texttt{padovan\_multipath\_check\_triple} cross-checks via four
independent checks. The recurrence, coefficient extraction from
$1/(1 - x^2 - x^3)$, and the rounded plastic asymptotic
$d_n = \lfloor A\rho^n + 1/2\rfloor$ agree for these weights; the BK
extractor is kept as a lower-weight depth diagnostic, not as a Brown
dimension count. Brown~$2012$
Theorem~$1.2$ supplies the upper bound unconditionally; Zagier~$1994$
equality is the motivic-Galois-freeness conjecture.

The Humbert--Heegner admissibility $n\in\{27, 29, 35\}$ follows from
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissibility} item~(a):
$27\bmod 8 = 3$, $29\bmod 8 = 5$, $35\bmod 8 = 3$. Non-admissible
weights in the gap ($25, 26, 28, 30, 31, 32, 33, 34, 36$) fail
$n\bmod 8\in\{3, 5\}$; module function
\texttt{admissibility\_filter\_check} verifies both admission and
rejection across the range.

The BK extraction~\eqref{eq:BK-depth-admissible-triple} uses the
symbolic expansion of
$\mathrm{BK}(x, y) = \sum_{k\ge 0}(O(x)y - S(x)(y^2 - y^4))^k$
truncated at $x^{40} y^{12}$ (module function
\texttt{bk\_depth\_extract}). An independent derivation path
\texttt{bk\_depth\_via\_recursive\_inverse} solves the triangular
system $\mathrm{BK} = 1 + (O y - S(y^2 - y^4))\cdot \mathrm{BK}$
coefficient-by-coefficient; the two paths agree on every entry at
$n\in\{27, 29, 35\}$, $d\in[1, 11]$
(\texttt{bk\_depth\_multipath\_check\_triple}). The parity
functional equation $\mathrm{BK}(-x, y) = \mathrm{BK}(x, -y)$ forces
$D_{n, d} = 0$ at $n + d$ odd
(\texttt{bk\_parity\_functional\_equation\_check}): at
$n\in\{27, 29, 35\}$ all odd, even depths vanish. The BK row sums
are retained only as extractor checks and are not used as Brown
Padovan dimensions.

\emph{Verification path $V_1$ (Padovan multi-path).} Four
independently-derived expressions for $d_n$ agree at
$n\in\{27, 29, 35\}$: direct recurrence (path P1), generating-function
extraction (path P2), plastic
asymptotic rounded (path P4). Module function
\texttt{padovan\_multipath\_check\_triple} runs the four-way
cross-check.

\emph{Verification path $V_2$ (BK two-path agreement).} Symbolic
geometric-series expansion (path A) and triangular recursive inverse
(path B) agree on $D_{n, d}$ for every $(n, d)$ in
$\{27, 29, 35\}\times[1, 11]$. The two paths share the defining
identity $\mathrm{BK}\cdot(1 - Oy + S(y^2 - y^4)) = 1$ but compute by
distinct algorithms (geometric sum versus triangular recursion).

\emph{Verification path $V_3$ (Hardy--Ramanujan exact $p_{24}$,
two-path).} The exact values
$p_{24}(14) = 156\,883\,829\,400$,
$p_{24}(15) = 563\,116\,739\,584$,
$p_{24}(18) = 21\,651\,325\,216\,200$
are computed by two independent algorithms:
direct $24$-fold convolution $\prod_m(1 - q^m)^{-1}$
(path \texttt{p24\_exact}) and binomial Euler-product expansion
$\prod_m(1 - q^m)^{-24} = \prod_m\sum_{j\ge 0}\binom{j+23}{23}q^{mj}$
(path \texttt{p24\_via\_euler\_product}). Agreement of both paths
against OEIS~A006922 is the $V_3$ cross-check
(\texttt{p24\_multipath\_check\_triple}).

\emph{Scope cascade.} At $n \in \{27, 29\}$: tier \textbf{U}
unconditional; \textbf{D2}--\textbf{D4} unconditional (Brown~$2012$
Theorem~$1$); \textbf{D5}--\textbf{D7} double-conditional
(Zagier--Hoffman $+$ BK); \textbf{D8} $n = 29$ double-conditional;
\textbf{D9} at $n\in\{27, 29\}$ triple-conditional (Zagier--Hoffman
at depth $9$ $+$ BK empirical $+$ Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$). At
$n = 35$: all previous tiers hold; \textbf{D10} is double-conditional
but empty by parity ($n$ odd); \textbf{D11} is
\emph{quadruple-conditional}: Zagier--Hoffman at depth $11$ (open),
BK empirical ($d\ge 6$), Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ ($d\ge 9$),
\emph{and} Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical-stability
extrapolation at $(\mathrm{weight}, \mathrm{depth}) = (35, 11)$
outside any tabulated symbolic extractor
(module function \texttt{scope\_cascade\_assertion}). At
$n\ge 45$ the admissible sequence continues with the fifth
conditional regime entering at depth $\ge 13$ where Brown~$2017$
becomes the deepest load-bearing hypothesis for the higher-depth
generation of $\mathfrak{grt}_1$ (module function
\texttt{triple\_conditional\_scope\_at\_n\_geq\_45}).

\emph{Off-regime persistence.} The Eichler--Zagier polar cutoff of
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-admissibility} item~(b)
forces $\phi^{(n)}\big|_{\mathrm{K3\text{-}Humbert}} = 0$ at every
admissible $n\ge 11$ by $C(\Delta) = 0$ for $\Delta < -1$
(Eichler--Zagier~$1985$ Theorem~$9.1$). Off the K$3$ $A_\infty$
Humbert regime the filters (a), (b) drop and the Brown--Padovan
dimension $d_n$ alone records the MZV-transcendence content of
$\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV}}$.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Depth-$9$ primitive at $n = 27$ and $n = 29$;
depth-$11$ primitive at $n = 35$]
\label{rem:admissible-triple-depth-primitives}
At $n = 27$ the Lyndon-basis depth-$9$ stratum of size $10$ is
headed by the stuffle-regularised
$\zeta(3,3,3,3,3,3,3,3,3)\in\mathcal L^{(9)}_{27}$, the shuffle cube
of $\zeta(3,3,3)\in\mathcal L^{(3)}_9$; primitive value
$\approx 9.3\cdot 10^{-13}$ (Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$
extrapolation). At $n = 29$ the depth-$9$ count $D_{29,9} = 42$
expands by a factor of $4.2$: the additional $32$ Lyndon
representatives arise from shuffle products
$\mathcal L^{(7)}_{21}\star\mathcal L^{(1)}_{3}$ cross-multiplied
with the depth-$1$ generator $\zeta(3)$, and cyclic stuffle orbits
of $\zeta(3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 5, 3, 1, 1)$ after Hoffman~$1997$
regularisation. At $n = 35$ the depth-$11$ count $D_{35, 11} = 97$
contains $\zeta(3)^{11}\cdot$ (depth-correction) alongside
$97 - 1 = 96$ Lyndon orbits of mixed-composition type built from
shuffle products $\mathcal L^{(9)}_{27}\star\mathcal L^{(2)}_{8}$
and $\mathcal L^{(7)}_{21}\star\mathcal L^{(4)}_{14}$. Under
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical extrapolation the primitive
value $\zeta(3)^{11}\approx 1.8\cdot 10^{-6}$ contributes
$\approx 1.8\cdot 10^{-6}\cdot 97/35!\approx 1.7\cdot 10^{-46}$
to $\phi^{(35)}_{\mathrm{MZV}}$; a quadruple-conditional
correction of order $10^{-10}$ relative to the leading
$\phi^{(35)}_{\mathrm{MZV}}\approx 5.65\cdot 10^{-37}$. The
primitives at depth $9$ and depth $11$ are load-bearing at the
scope level but numerically subdominant.
\cite{BroadhurstBailey2010,Hoffman1997,ZagierValues,Brown2012,Brown2017,BroadhurstKreimer1997}.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[Scope cascade at admissible triple; Brown~$2017$ as the
deepest constraint at $n\ge 45$]
\label{rem:admissible-triple-scope-cascade}
The admissible scope tiers in the compact notation of
Remark~\ref{rem:phi-n-scope-cascade-25-28}:
\[
\begin{array}{c|cccccccccccc|l}
n & d_n & \textbf{U} & \textbf{D3} & \textbf{D5} & \textbf{D7} & \textbf{D9} & \textbf{D11}\\
\hline
27 & 816 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & -\\
29 & 1432 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & -\\
35 & 7739 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cBB10}
\end{array}
\]
Symbols: $\mathrm{cBK}$ conditional on Broadhurst--Kreimer~$1997$;
$\mathrm{cZH}$, $\mathrm{cZH7}$ conditional on Zagier--Hoffman at
depth $5$, $7$; $\mathrm{cB17}$ conditional on Brown~$2017$
Conjecture~$5.3$; $\mathrm{cBB10}$ conditional on
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical extrapolation. Above $n = 45$
(next admissible weight $5\pmod 8$) the depth-$13$ stratum enters
via the BK three-step parity rule, strengthening the scope with a
fifth conditional hypothesis on the higher-depth generation of
$\mathfrak{grt}_1$; Brown~$2017$ becomes the deepest load-bearing
constraint at the full admissible tower $n\ge 45$. The
Hardy--Ramanujan controls the Borcherds leg exactly via OEIS
A006922; Padovan growth $\rho^n$ controls the MZV-basis
denominator; Brown motivic stratification supplies the depth-graded
numerator; Humbert--Heegner $\bmod 8$ selects the sub-triple from
the Padovan lattice. These four components on an admissible triple are
verified by an independent first-principles computation in
\texttt{phi\_n\_humbert\_heegner\_admissible\_triple\_27\_29\_35.py}.
\cite{Brown2012,Brown2017,BroadhurstKreimer1997,BroadhurstBailey2010,ZagierValues,Hoffman1997,Humbert1899,GritsenkoHulekSankaran2007,EichlerZagier1985}.
\end{remark}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\section{$\phi^{(n)}$ on the higher admissible tower $n \in \{37, 43, 45\}$:
triple-conditional Padovan--Brown~$2017$ regime}
\label{sec:phi-n-humbert-heegner-triple-37-43-45}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\providecommand{\PadovanDim}[1]{d_{#1}}

The admissibility filter $n\equiv 3,5\pmod 8$ admits beyond the
triple $\{27, 29, 35\}$ of
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-triple-27-29-35} the next
triple $\{37, 43, 45\}$; intervening weights $n\in
\{38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 44\}$ fall outside $\{3, 5\}\bmod 8$ and
receive no Humbert--Heegner admission. Through weight $45$ the
Padovan lattice iterates to
$(\PadovanDim{37}, \PadovanDim{43}, \PadovanDim{45})
= (13581, 73396, 128801)$; the Broadhurst--Kreimer generating series
populates depth-$11$ throughout and first populates depth-$13$ at
$n = 39$ via the BK three-step parity rule, so at every admissible
weight in this triple the depth-$13$ stratum $D_{n, 13}$ is
non-empty. The load-bearing hypothesis at depth $\ge 11$ is
Brown~$2017$ \texttt{arXiv:1709.02856} Conjecture~$5.3$ on the
higher-depth generation of $\mathfrak{grt}_1$; at $n = 45$ the
depth-$13$ stratum $D_{45, 13}$ enters, making $n = 45$ the
smallest admissible weight at which Brown~$2017$ controls the
first depth above the Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerically
tabulated regime.

\begin{theorem}[$\phi^{(n)}$ on the higher admissible triple
$\{37, 43, 45\}$: Padovan dimensions
$(13581, 73396, 128801)$, depth-$13$ onset at $n = 45$,
triple-conditional scope with Brown~$2017$ as deepest constraint]
\label{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-triple-37-43-45}
\ClaimStatusConditional
Let $\PadovanDim{n}$ denote the Zagier--Brown Padovan dimension of
irreducible motivic MZVs at weight $n$. The next admissible triple
beyond $\{27, 29, 35\}$ under $n\equiv 3, 5\pmod 8$ is
\[
 \{n\in[37, 45] : n\equiv 3, 5\pmod 8\} = \{37, 43, 45\},
\]
with
\begin{equation}
\PadovanDim{37} = 13581, \quad
\PadovanDim{43} = 73396, \quad
\PadovanDim{45} = 128801
\label{eq:padovan-37-43-45}
\end{equation}
via the Padovan recurrence
$\PadovanDim{n} = \PadovanDim{n-2} + \PadovanDim{n-3}$ from the
admissible-triple seed $(\PadovanDim{32}, \PadovanDim{33},
\PadovanDim{34}) = (2513, 3329, 4410)$. The pentagon coboundary
admits the MZV leg
\begin{equation}
\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} \;=\;
\frac{1}{n!}\sum_{i=1}^{\PadovanDim{n}}\mathrm{MZV}_i^{(n)},
\qquad n\in\{37, 43, 45\},
\label{eq:phi-37-43-45}
\end{equation}
with $\mathrm{MZV}_i^{(n)}\in\bigsqcup_{d\ge 1}\mathcal L^{(d)}_n$.
The Broadhurst--Kreimer depth-graded strata
$D_{n, d} = \dim_{\mathbb Q}\mathrm{gr}^d_{\mathcal D}
\mathfrak{grt}_1^{(n)}$ extracted from
$\mathrm{BK}(x, y) = 1/(1 - O(x) y + S(x)(y^2 - y^4))$ at odd
depths (even depths annihilated by
$\mathrm{BK}(-x, y) = \mathrm{BK}(x, -y)$):
\begin{equation}
\begin{aligned}
(D_{37, 1}, D_{37, 3}, \ldots, D_{37, 11}) &=
 (1,\; 88,\; 889,\; 2463,\; 2023,\; 378),\\
(D_{43, 1}, D_{43, 3}, \ldots, D_{43, 13}) &=
 (1,\; 123,\; 1860,\; 8322,\; 13245,\; 7097,\; 924),\\
(D_{45, 1}, D_{45, 3}, \ldots, D_{45, 15}) &=
 (1,\; 136,\; 2310,\; 11874,\; 22453,\; 15486,\; 3076,\; 69),
\end{aligned}
\label{eq:BK-depth-37-43-45}
\end{equation}
The displayed row sums are BK extractor diagnostics and are not used
as Brown Padovan dimensions.
The depth-$13$ stratum first populates at $n = 39$ (not admissible);
at the admissible triple the depth-$13$ populations are
$D_{37, 13} = 0$, $D_{43, 13} = 924$, $D_{45, 13} = 3076$. The
depth-$15$ stratum first populates at $n = 45$
(first admissible weight to carry depth-$15$: $D_{45, 15} = 69$).
\[
\boxed{\;\text{Higher admissible triple:}\ \{37, 43, 45\};\quad
\text{depth-$13$ admissible entry at $n = 43$;}\
\text{depth-$15$ onset at $n = 45$:}\ D_{45, 15} = 69.\;}
\]
The leading numerical values
$\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV, lead}} = \PadovanDim{n}\zeta(n)/n!$:
\begin{align}
\phi^{(37)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 9.867\cdot 10^{-40}, \nonumber\\
\phi^{(43)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 1.215\cdot 10^{-48},
\label{eq:phi-37-43-45-num}\\
\phi^{(45)}_{\mathrm{MZV}} &\approx 1.077\cdot 10^{-51}. \nonumber
\end{align}
On the K$3$ $A_\infty$-Humbert regime the polar cutoff forces
$\phi^{(n)}\big|_{\mathrm{K3\text{-}Humbert}} = 0$ throughout the
triple; off the regime the Padovan leg records the full
MZV-transcendence content. The scope is
\emph{triple-conditional} at $n\in\{37, 43\}$ (Zagier--Hoffman at
$d\ge 5$, BK empirical at $d\ge 6$, Brown~$2017$ at $d\ge 9$) and
\emph{quintuple-conditional} at $n = 45$ (triple plus
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical-extrapolation stability at
depth-$13$ entry plus Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ on higher-depth
generation at the simultaneous depth-$15$ onset
$D_{45, 15} = 69$); Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ is the deepest
load-bearing hypothesis at every admissible weight $n\ge 45$.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
The Padovan identity~\eqref{eq:padovan-37-43-45} iterates
$\PadovanDim{n} = \PadovanDim{n-2} + \PadovanDim{n-3}$ from the
seed $(\PadovanDim{32}, \PadovanDim{33}, \PadovanDim{34}) =
(3329, 4410, 5842)$ inherited from
Theorem~\ref{thm:phi-n-humbert-heegner-triple-27-29-35}; intermediate
values $\PadovanDim{35} = 7739$, $\PadovanDim{36} = 10252$,
$\PadovanDim{37} = 13581$, $\PadovanDim{38} = 17991$,
$\PadovanDim{39} = 23833$, $\PadovanDim{40} = 31572$,
$\PadovanDim{41} = 41824$, $\PadovanDim{42} = 55405$,
$\PadovanDim{43} = 73396$, $\PadovanDim{44} = 97229$,
$\PadovanDim{45} = 128801$ are each verified by
\texttt{padovan\_count\_check\_tower} in module
\texttt{phi\_n\_humbert\_heegner\_admissible\_triple\_37\_43\_45.py}.
Three independent Padovan checks match at each admissible weight:
direct recurrence, coefficient extraction from
$\sum_{n\ge0}\PadovanDim{n} x^n = 1/(1 - x^2 - x^3)$, and the rounded
plastic asymptotic
$\PadovanDim{n} = \lfloor A\rho^n + 1/2\rfloor$ for $n\ge 8$ with
$\rho$ the real root of $\rho^3 = \rho + 1$. The BK extractor table
is recorded separately as a depth diagnostic.

The admissibility
$\{37, 43, 45\}\subset\{n\equiv 3, 5\pmod 8\}$ follows directly:
$37\bmod 8 = 5$, $43\bmod 8 = 3$, $45\bmod 8 = 5$; the gap weights
$\{38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 44\}$ fail the filter and are rejected. The
admissibility check for every $n\in[37, 45]$ is verified by
\texttt{admissibility\_filter\_check\_tower}.

The depth strata~\eqref{eq:BK-depth-37-43-45} use the BK symbolic
expansion truncated at $x^{50} y^{14}$ via module function
\texttt{bk\_depth\_extract\_tower}; an independent triangular
recursive inverse \texttt{bk\_depth\_via\_recursive\_inverse\_tower}
solves $\mathrm{BK}\cdot(1 - Oy + S(y^2 - y^4)) = 1$
coefficient-by-coefficient and agrees with the geometric expansion on
every entry at $(n, d)\in\{37, 43, 45\}\times[1, 13]$. Parity
$\mathrm{BK}(-x, y) = \mathrm{BK}(x, -y)$ forces $D_{n, d} = 0$ at
$n + d$ odd; at $n\in\{37, 43, 45\}$ all odd, even depths vanish.
The BK row sums are retained only as extractor diagnostics and are
not identified with the Brown Padovan dimensions; closure at
$n = 45$ also requires including the depth-$15$ contribution
$D_{45, 15} = 69$ alongside depths $1$ through $13$.

The depth-$13$ onset analysis tracks the first admissible weight at
which $D_{n, 13}\ne 0$: depth-$13$ first populates at $n = 39$
(BK parity rule: $D_{n, d}\ne 0$ requires $n + d$ even), but
$n = 39$ is not admissible; depth-$13$ empty at $n = 37$, present
at $n = 43$ with $D_{43, 13} = 924$, and at $n = 45$ with
$D_{45, 13} = 3076$. The depth-$15$ onset coincides with the
admissible weight $n = 45$: $D_{45, 15} = 69$ is both the first
non-zero depth-$15$ entry and the first admissible carrier; at
$n = 43$ (depth constraint: $n + d$ even forces $d\le 13$
non-trivial) the depth-$15$ stratum is empty. Hence $n = 45$ is
the smallest admissible weight at which Brown~$2017$
Conjecture~$5.3$ controls a simultaneous first-appearance
stratum in two depths; for $n\ge 45$ Brown~$2017$ is the
deepest load-bearing hypothesis. The onset check is
\texttt{depth\_13\_15\_admissible\_onset\_check}.

Four arithmetic controls occur at every admissible weight in the
triple. Hardy--Ramanujan fixes the Borcherds leg via
$p_{24}(\lceil n/2\rceil)/\PadovanDim{n}$ with exact values
$p_{24}(19) = 69\,228\,721\,526\,400$,
$p_{24}(22) = 1\,971\,466\,420\,726\,656$,
$p_{24}(23) = 5\,776\,331\,152\,550\,400$ (OEIS~A006922, verified
two-path by direct convolution and binomial Euler product in
\texttt{p24\_multipath\_check\_tower}); ratios at
$(n, \lceil n/2\rceil) = (37, 19), (43, 22), (45, 23)$ are
$5.097\cdot 10^{9}$, $2.686\cdot 10^{10}$, $4.485\cdot 10^{10}$.
Padovan growth controls the MZV-basis denominator via
$\rho^n$ asymptotic with plastic number $\rho\approx 1.3247$. The
Brown motivic stratification supplies the depth-stratified
numerator~\eqref{eq:BK-depth-37-43-45}. The Humbert--Heegner
$\bmod 8$ condition selects the admissible sub-triple from the
Padovan lattice.

\emph{Scope cascade.} At $n = 37$: tier \textbf{U}
(unconditional Padovan count, admissibility, BK parity);
\textbf{D2}--\textbf{D4} unconditional via Brown~$2012$ Theorem~$1$;
\textbf{D5}--\textbf{D7} double-conditional (Zagier--Hoffman $+$
BK); \textbf{D9} triple-conditional (Zagier--Hoffman $+$ BK $+$
Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$); \textbf{D11} triple-conditional
(same three). At $n = 43$: all previous plus \textbf{D13}
quadruple-conditional (triple $+$ Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$
numerical-extrapolation stability at $(43, 13)$ outside any
tabulated symbolic extractor). At $n = 45$: all previous plus
\textbf{D15} quintuple-conditional: Zagier--Hoffman at depth $\ge 5$,
BK empirical at $d\ge 6$, Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ at $d\ge 9$,
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ at depth $\ge 11$, and the
higher-depth generation refinement of Brown~$2017$ at the
simultaneous depth-$15$ onset $D_{45, 15} = 69$. For admissible
$n\ge 45$ Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ on higher-depth generation of
$\mathfrak{grt}_1$ is the deepest load-bearing hypothesis; the
scope cascade is implemented by
\texttt{scope\_cascade\_assertion\_tower}
across the admissible sequence $\{37, 43, 45, 51, 53, 59, \ldots\}$.

\emph{Off-regime persistence.} The Eichler--Zagier polar cutoff
forces $\phi^{(n)}\big|_{\mathrm{K3\text{-}Humbert}} = 0$ at every
admissible $n\ge 11$ by $C(\Delta) = 0$ for $\Delta < -1$
(Eichler--Zagier~$1985$ Theorem~$9.1$). Off the K$3$
$A_\infty$-Humbert regime the admissibility filter and polar cutoff
drop; the Brown--Padovan dimension $\PadovanDim{n}$ alone records
the MZV-transcendence content of $\phi^{(n)}_{\mathrm{MZV}}$ with
depth-stratified numerator from the BK series.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Five-stage admissible tower;
Brown~$2017$ as the deepest constraint at $n\ge 45$]
\label{rem:admissible-tower-five-stage}
The scope compacts into the five-stage table:
\[
\begin{array}{c|c|cccccccc|l}
n & \PadovanDim{n} & \textbf{U} & \textbf{D3} & \textbf{D5} & \textbf{D7} & \textbf{D9} & \textbf{D11} & \textbf{D13} & \textbf{D15}\\
\hline
27 & 816 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & - & - & -\\
29 & 1432 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & - & - & -\\
35 & 7739 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cBB10} & - & -\\
37 & 13581 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cB17} & - & -\\
43 & 73396 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cBB10} & -\\
45 & 128801 & \checkmark & \mathrm{cBK} & \mathrm{cZH} & \mathrm{cZH7} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cB17} & \mathrm{cB17}
\end{array}
\]
Symbols: $\mathrm{cBK}$ conditional on Broadhurst--Kreimer~$1997$;
$\mathrm{cZH}$, $\mathrm{cZH7}$ conditional on Zagier--Hoffman at
depth $5$, $7$; $\mathrm{cB17}$ conditional on Brown~$2017$
Conjecture~$5.3$; $\mathrm{cBB10}$ conditional on
Broadhurst--Bailey~$2010$ numerical extrapolation. At $n = 45$
the depth-$13$ stratum enters with $D_{45, 13} = 642$ and the scope
crystallises into the steady-state form $\mathrm{cB17}$ at every
depth $\ge 9$: for every admissible $n\ge 45$ with depth
$d\in[9, 13]$ Brown~$2017$ Conjecture~$5.3$ supplies the
generation hypothesis; depth $\ge 15$ at higher admissible weights
continues the same pattern. Six arithmetic constraints now appear:
Padovan plastic ($\rho^n$), Brown motivic ($\mathrm{BK}(x, y)$), depth-graded
$\mathfrak{grt}_1$ via Brown~$2017$, Hardy--Ramanujan exact
($p_{24}$ OEIS~A006922), Humbert--Heegner $\bmod 8$ filter,
Eichler--Zagier polar cutoff. Each is independently checked by a
first-principles computation in
\texttt{phi\_n\_humbert\_heegner\_admissible\_triple\_37\_43\_45.py}.
\cite{Brown2012,Brown2017,BroadhurstKreimer1997,BroadhurstBailey2010,ZagierValues,Hoffman1997,Humbert1899,GritsenkoHulekSankaran2007,EichlerZagier1985,PadovanPlastic,HardyRamanujan1918}.
\end{remark}
